F10:0015                                       ; format 04 value.b, where value equals value*tilewidth=8 pixels
F10:0016

F10:0018       cc_jump             equ $06     ; Jumps to a text location
F10:0019                                       ; format: 06.b pointer.w

F13:0006       textData_Dialogues:
F13:0007       
F13:0008       ; First textbox that pops up automatically upon game start in the house
F13:0009       text1: 
F13:0010           ;                                      left    margins
F13:0011           ;                                      ^       ^
F13:0012           dc.b $0B,$11,$10,$00,$A5,$03,$06,$0A,$01,$04,$01,$07
               S49:000A4F9D:  0B
               S49:000A4F9E:  11
               S49:000A4F9F:  10
               S49:000A4FA0:  00
               S49:000A4FA1:  A5
               S49:000A4FA2:  03
               S49:000A4FA3:  06
               S49:000A4FA4:  0A
               S49:000A4FA5:  01
               S49:000A4FA6:  04
               S49:000A4FA7:  01
               S49:000A4FA8:  07
F13:0013           ; Monster World war|einst ein friedvoller|Ort.
F13:0014           dc.b $0C,$54," ",$0C,$67," war",cc_newline,"einst ein friedvoller",cc_newline,"Ort."
